[30;1m1349 | [0m[35m#### Named escape markup: `@\^{...}`[0m
[30;1m1350 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m1351 | [0m[35mThe escape markup for controls `@\^...` has an extended usage where[0m
[30;1m1352 | [0m[35mthe character can be specified by a control code name.  The resulting[0m
[30;1m1353 | [0m[35m**named escape markup** takes the form of `@\^{...}` with the escape[0m
[30;1m1354 | [0m[35mcode name between the curly braces.  The name of the escape code used[0m
[30;1m1355 | [0m[35min the markup is case insensitive.[0m

[30;1m990 | [0m[35mA trailing prefix after markup which has beginning and ending[0m
[30;1m991 | [0m[35mdelimiters -- for instance, inline comment (`@*...*`), expression[0m

[30;1m994 | [0m[35mof the line after the markup.  The trailing prefix will consume the[0m
[30;1m995 | [0m[35mfinal newline, eliminating unwanted newlines.[0m
